 This is a  list of cards in  Yu-Gi-Oh! BAM . The game features 1068 playable cards after the  Chapter 8 Qualifications  update on November 13, 2013 and occasionally receives updates that add additional cards.

 Changes 
 Main article:  List of Yu-Gi-Oh! BAM cards/Changes 
 Bugs 
 The effect of " Elemental HERO Bladedge " boosts all monsters. (Fixed on July 10, 2013) 
 " Hieratic Seal of the Sun Dragon Overlord " only annihilates its opponent's Dark Monsters, not "all Dark Monsters" as mentioned in the text. (Fixed on September 25, 2013)
 However, a new bug was created. When a non-Dark Monster is destroyed at the same time as that Dark Monster (e.g.  Vampire's Curse  was destroyed), "Hieratic Seal of the Sun Dragon Overlord" will also count those monsters and further increase Life Points. 
 It is not known if the following are bugs, or if it was intended, but they do not follow their text. 
 The effect of " Aurkus, Lightsworn Druid " and " Hieratic Dragon of Nuit " ignores player priority and activates before " Evolsaur Darwino ", unlike other Immune All [Type] cards. 
 The effect of " Skilled White Magician " activates at Round Start, before " Toy Magician " and " Endymion, the Master Magician " (Annihilate). 
 " Dark Magician of Chaos " grants Immunity even if a Spell is destroyed in the same channel. 
 The following are known bugs. 
 Photon Wyvern  will not boost or increase your Life Points if it is in the 2nd or 3rd column. 
 Blackback  activates whenever your monster gains Power, not just once when Blackback activates. So if a player uses a Drain or Empathy Winged Beast monster, it will create an loop to OTK the opponent. (Fixed on October 9, 2013)
